msg:The Marriott hotel in Yantai is one of the best hotels in Yantai. It has an incredible view of the ocean, and sits on the ocean boardwalk, making it very easy to go for morning runs or evening strolls.

The hotel uses many light colors in its decorations so the hotel and the rooms feel open and bright. The atmosphere is calm and peaceful. 

The rooms are clean, and the beds are comfortable everything you would expect from a Marriott hotel .

Unfortunately, the room was a bit cold. I had to wear long sleeves and a jacket in the room. Also, except for the amazing omelettes, the breakfast is lacking.

But I have stayed at the Yantai Marriott in the past and will stay there again in the future.

msg:This place is a real gem. Yantai city is not the most interesting place to visit, but if you are looking for a private, relaxing, and pampering experience, this hotel will satisfy those needs while not costing a fortune. The queen room we originally booked was not suitable and I wouldn‚Äôt recommend it. The bathroom is not separated from the bedroom by a real wall, and instead uses a ‚Äúprivacy screen‚Äù to obscure a direct view of the toilet. This of course helps to make the room appear bigger in photos. We immediately upgraded to the suite which was a massive improvement for only a couple hundred RMB more, which was comped by daily access to the executive lounge where buffet dinner and alcoholic drinks were served. Location is amazing. The new economic zone is arguably prettier than either penglai or Yantai. The beach is pristine, and seemingly is only used by hotel guests. Several acres of scrub forest divide the hotel from the main roads, giving you a feeling of real isolation from the outside world, and in China that‚Äôs very rare. Staff were great. Room was always clean. Food and services were on point. Would book again!

The front desk said that we could not be transferred because there were too many guests in the hotel, so we had to give up. When we opened the door and entered the guest room, it happened that the hotel room manager Shi Yaxing came to greet us and delivered snacks and drinks. At this time, we mentioned the room arrangement to Manager Shi Yaxing. Manager Shi immediately said that she would coordinate the matter. In a short time, Manager Shi arranged the room transfer properly and transferred the 11th floor room to the 15th floor, so that our family could take care of each other very conveniently. During the stay in the hotel, Manager Shi was also responsive to all requests and questions, and personally arranged for us to extend our stay. msg:Traveling with a baby (the baby is only one year and eight months old), we were told that the room had no balcony when we checked in the executive twin room we booked, and then we paid the difference to upgrade to an executive room with a balcony. The balcony faces the sea and the view is pretty good, but the room area is not very large and the balcony is relatively small. We informed the check-in staff in advance that we needed to arrange a quieter room. It was inconvenient to bring a baby and we were afraid of affecting others, but we still arranged it next to the executive lounge, which was not very satisfactory. Later, the administrative lady said that we would arrange a change, but the baby had too much luggage and was too lazy to change. Fortunately, there were not many people in the executive lounge and the noise was not very loud. The babies slept well at night. There was no baby fence, and the staff helped to move the chairs to block it.
The room card took a long time to get on the first day of check-in. We took the baby to lunch and urged for a long time before it was delivered. The experience was not very good. (Lunch is Cantonese dim sum on the second floor, fortunately it is relatively light, rice noodle rolls, beef balls and wontons can be eaten together by the dolls, chicken feet and spare ribs are relatively hard and not soft)
The executive lounge has light meals and afternoon tea in the morning and evening, with quite a lot of varieties and they are all very light. Bring the dolls here to eat some fruit before going out after waking up. Three meals can basically be solved here. Clean and hygienic, it solves the most headache problem for mothers, and the children can eat with peace of mind. In addition, the ladies in the executive lounge are very enthusiastic, especially Miss Anna, who smiles and speaks very gently every day, and her mood will be better when she sees them. She will help the dolls to get up when they fall down, and give them snacks every time she sees the babies, and patiently prepare warm water for the dolls. The two children chase after them every day and call Aunt Meimei. They really like the aunts. After dinner, they rest on the sofa and let the dolls play by themselves, which is super worry-free.
It is a three-minute walk to the beach. There is a foot bath downstairs of the hotel. The front desk provides sand digging tools, which is very user-friendly. There is a small children's play area on the second floor of the hotel, which is a bit too small for us and suitable for younger babies.
The hotel is a six-minute taxi ride away from AEON, where food, drinks and entertainment are quite complete. It is a ten-minute taxi ride away from the lonely whale check-in point, and there is an outdoor children's play area on the left.
Overall, this trip was quite pleasant, and the most satisfying thing was the service staff in the executive lounge. All mothers with children must upgrade their room types.

msg:"Affordable" Marriott with ocean view~

When booking a room, I also looked at the Hilton and Westin near Golden Beach. They are all hotels under the same group, and I finally chose this one because I like the Marriott's ocean-view terrace.

This Marriott is located near the development zone, 30 minutes from the airport and about 40 minutes from the city. Please be careful when taking photos here.

The lady at the front desk who checked in was very enthusiastic and helped me change to the room type I liked. Special mention goes to Devie Liu~ she is kind and kind. She helped me carry my luggage and walked me to the elevator.

When we arrived at the room, it happened to be low tide, and we could see people rushing to the beach from the balcony... It was very lively, the sea water was clear, and the beach was very clean... It's very suitable for taking children to play ~

The room is quite satisfactory, the quality that Marriott should have. But the restaurant is very artistic... There are three small bubble-style outdoor private rooms on the square downstairs. At night, with the lights on the square, it is very artistic. The restaurant also has a seat overlooking the sea indoors. The dishes are very rich and are a combination of Chinese and Western. There are pizza, pasta, and Yantai special fried shrimp cakes...

I highly recommend this affordable Marriott hotel with a view of the sea. It is a good choice whether you are traveling for business or vacation!

msg:Every parent-child outing, choose five-star hotels as much as possible. When you come to Yantai during the Dragon Boat Festival holiday, you should first consider the surrounding environment. It is the Golden Beach. There are three 5-star hotels in Golden Beach, Hilton, Marriott, and Sheraton. Decisively choose Marriott. I used my spouse‚Äôs Marriott member to book a luxury double, plus a service fee of about 795. I accidentally found that Ctrip had booked 719. I booked it for 4 days and 3 nights with Ctrip. I arrived at the hotel at around 6:30 pm on the first day of the long vacation. The child was in the car. I fell asleep, and I couldn‚Äôt drive the door with my baby in my arms. My wife wanted to take a bag and a suitcase. The doorman standing next to us was standing there watching us. He didn‚Äôt mean to step forward and help. Instead, the special car driver came down to help. We, this point is really deducted. If it is left in the past, the child is awake, I will pull the child with the bag, and the husband pulls the luggage. It is completely ok!
When I checked in, I informed that there were children and breakfast was only two mornings. Whether it was possible to send breakfast for a child, the little brother at the front desk was very embarrassed to consider it for a while and agreed. When I arrived in the room, there was dust on the table in the room, hair on the bedding, and stains on the toilet cover. Wipe it off with the alcohol cotton pad I brought. For breakfast, due to the small holiday, it was a little more than 8 o'clock in the morning for two consecutive days, and we had to wait in line. The dishes are slightly less, and the fried stuff is the majority. The oil is too big and very greasy. The only vegetables in the stir-fry are broccoli, garlic moss, and baby vegetables. There are only lettuce, carrots, and onions in the vegetable salad. In a five-star hotel in a coastal city, there is no seafood for breakfast, not even a small shrimp. Well, I can only comfort myself, there are so many small long dummy, the restaurant is too busy.
The hotel tends to be business-oriented, and the parent-child travel experience is average, especially with younger children. It is inconvenient to go to the toilet and wash. In the past, five-star hotels in other cities will have children‚Äôs toilets, and there will be a non-slip stool under the washbasin, which is convenient for children to stand there to wash. These days, adults have to hold or hold their armpits when children go to the toilet. The toilet is small, and the toilet is large. If you don‚Äôt support it, you will fall into it. You have to hold your hands to wash your hands. One person helps the child wash. When showering, there are no bathroom slippers in the bathroom. Adults stand barefoot and slip inside. , I hope that the hotel can consider some children's factors in it. After all, there are not a few families with children on long vacations, winter and summer vacations.
In addition, the advantage of the hotel is that the decoration is relatively modern. Each room has a large balcony with good lighting and ventilation. The climate in Yantai is very good. Although it is close to the sea, it is not humid. The back door of the hotel is a beach with few people and quiet!
Next time I come to Yantai, I will choose Marriott. I hope that the details of the hotel will get better and better.
